촊PART 4 — UNIFIED DATA MODEL (UDM): CORE REPRESENTATION (Detailed PRD)촚Master Structural + Architectural + Estimation + Work?ow + Project Management Data Model촪This part de?nes the single source of truth for the entire application—from concept → architectural layout → structural model → analysis → design → estimation → execution → closure 촺It is the backbone that makes the app behave like a fusion of:쵊•쵚STAAD / ETABS / Robot Structural Analysis / Tekla (structural modeling + analysis)쵪•쵺Revit / AutoCAD Architecture (architectural layouts + parametric modeling)춊•춚CPWD/State SSR Estimation Engines촐?•촑?Primavera/MSP-like Work?ows촒?•촓?BIM-enabled lifecycle management촔?Everything ?ows through this UDM 촕?촖촗?촘?4 1 Objectives of the Uni?ed Data Model촙?The UDM must:촠?1 촡?Represent ANY structure type촢?o촣?RCC buildings (G+1 to G+40)촤?o촥?Steel buildings / PEB촦?o촧?Industrial sheds촨?o촩?Retaining walls촰?o촱?RE walls촲?o촳?Land?lls촴?o촵?Water tanks촶?o촷?Compound walls촸?o촹?Foundations쵀?o쵁?Staircases쵂?o쵃?Bridges (future)쵄?o쵅?Roads (future)쵆?2 쵇?Be fully parametric쵈?o쵉?Editable like STAAD쵐?o쵑?Re-generatable layouts쵒?o쵓?Auto-update drawings A quantities on every change쵔?3 쵕?Enable AI-driven re?nement쵖?o쵗?The user says: “G+8 building in Hyderabad”쵘?o쵙?AI expands → UDM → model builder → design → drawings → quantities쵠?4 쵡?Unify structural + architectural + MEP placeholders(Even if MEP is a placeholder for Phase-1)쵢?5 쵣?Allow modular monetization쵤?o쵥?Architectural only쵦?o쵧?Structural design only쵨?o쵩?Estimation only쵰?o쵱?Execution management only쵲?o쵳?Full package (discounted)쵴?o쵵?Add-on services (peer review/ expert assistance/ permit set)쵶?쵷쵸?

촊DETAILED PRD — PART 4촚UNIFIED DATA MODEL (UDM) A STRUCTURAL DIGITAL TWIN CORE**촪This section de?nes the single source of truth for every building/structure the system handles Everything the system does—AI reasoning/ layout generation/ design/ analysis/ estimation/ drawings/ scheduling—depends on this UDM 촺This is the heart of the entire app 쵊?쵪쵺4 1 Purpose of the UDM춊The Uni?ed Data Model (UDM) acts as:춚•촐?The digital twin of the project촑?•촒?The master container for all inputs/ derived data/ analysis artefacts/ results/ and documents촓?•촔?A schema-driven layer that ensures consistency across all modules:촕?o촖?AI Conversational Input Engine촗?o촘?Architectural Layout Engine촙?o촠?Structural Modeling Engine촡?o촢?Analysis Engine (Kratos / FEniCSx / OpenSeesPy future support)촣?o촤?Design Engine (IS/ACI/AISC/EC)촥?o촦?Estimation Engine (SSR/state SOR/ CPWD/ AP/TG/KA/MH/DELHI SOR)촧?o촨?Drawings Engine (AutoCAD/DXF/SVG)촩?o촰?Project Execution Engine (Schedules/ BOQ integration)촱?The UDM ensures any structure type can be de?ned using one backbone 촲?촳촴?촵?4 2 Core Concepts촶?The UDM is composed of three layers:촷?촸촹?쵀?Layer A — User Intent A AI Normalization Layer쵁?This layer captures natural language inputs and converts them into structured context 쵂?Example input:쵃?“Construction of G+2 building in Hyderabad”쵄?AI normalizes into:쵅?{쵆? 촊PART 0 — MODEL ENTITIES A RELATIONSHIPS (MER)촚Master PRD for the AI-Driven Structural Design/ Estimation A Construction Management Platform촪?쵊쵚0 1  PURPOSE OF THIS SECTION쵪This section de?nes:쵺a) ALL fundamental engineering entities춊(beams/ columns/ slabs/ foundations/ walls/ frames/ nodes/ loads/ materials/ etc )춚b) ALL architectural/interior entities촐?(rooms/ walls/ openings/ furniture zones/ shafts/ circulation/ etc )촑?c) Non-structural but essential project elements촒?(?oors/ zones/ grids/ levels/ utility networks/ work?ows/ tasks/ cost objects)촓?d) Their relationships촔?(how beams attach to nodes/ how slabs sit on beams/ how walls attach to slabs/ how spaces relate to ?oors/ how drawings map to entities)촕?e) Shared data de?nitions A rules촖?(ID formats/ units/ metadata/ revisioning system/ inheritance/ validation rules)촗?This MER becomes the Universal Data Model (UDM) that every module can rely on 촘?촙촠?촡?0 2  UNIVERSAL OBJECT MODEL (UOM)촢?The UOM is a multi-hierarchical/ graph-based object model designed to support:촣?•촤?AI-driven design촥?•촦?Parametric modeling촧?•촨?FEM simulation촩?•촰?Architectural + structural collaboration촱?•촲?Quantity takeo?촳?•촴?Estimation촵?•촶?Scheduling촷?•촸?Approvals촹?•쵀?Revisions쵁?•쵂?Exports (DWG/ IFC/ DXF/ STAAD/ Kratos/ etc )쵃?쵄쵅?쵆?0 3  TOP-LEVEL CATEGORIES OF ENTITIES쵇?The entire platform has 5 primary classes of entities:쵈?쵉쵐?쵑?0 3 1  Project Domain Entities쵒?Entity쵓?Purpose쵔?Project쵕?Top-level container for all operations쵖?User / Roles / Permissions쵗?Organizations/ teams/ designers/ contractors쵘?Site쵙?GIS location/ climate/ wind/ seismic zone/ soil data쵠?Building / Facility쵡?A project may have multiple buildings쵢?Phase/Package쵣?Excavation/ structure/ MEP/ ?nishing쵤?쵥쵦?쵧?0 3 2  Architectural Domain Entities쵨?These support planning/ layouts/ space programming 
촊Entity촚Description촪Floor / Level촺Each storey with elevation쵊Grid System쵚A-B-C / 1-2-3 grid lines쵪Space / Room쵺Bedroom/ kitchen/ toilets/ corridors춊Architectural Wall춚Partition/ load-bearing/ non-load bearing촐?Opening촑?Doors/ windows/ ventilators촒?Staircase / Ramps촓?Geometric parameters촔?Shafts촕?Plumbing/ electrical/ AC shaft촖?Roof / Terrace촗?Sloped or ?at roof촘?Circulation Zones촙?Lift lobby/ corridors촠?촡촢?촣?0 3 3  Structural Domain Entities촤?These are core for analysis/ design/ and detailing 촥?Primary Structural Entities촦?Entity촧?Meaning촨?Node촩?FEM node with coordinates촰?Element촱?Frame/beam/column/plate/solid촲?Beam element촳?1D element촴?Column element촵?1D vertical element촶?Slab element촷?2D element촸?Wall element촹?2D vertical element쵀?Footing / Foundation쵁?Isolated/ combined/ strip/ raft쵂?Pile / Pile Cap쵃?Deep foundation entities쵄?Frame쵅?A collection of connected beams/columns쵆?Truss/Roof Frame쵇?PEB rafters/ purlins/ bracings쵈?Secondary Structural Entities쵉?Entity쵐?Description쵑?Bracing쵒?X-bracing/ K-bracing/ portal brace쵓?Tie Beams쵔?Plinth beams/ grade beams쵕?Lintels쵖?Over openings쵗?Retaining Wall쵘?Cantilever / Counterfort쵙?RE Wall쵠?Reinforced earth wall systems쵡?Land?ll Bund / Berm쵢?Geometric entities쵣?Slope / Embankment쵤?For retaining or land?ll쵥?쵦쵧?쵨?0 3 4  Material and Section Entities쵩?Materials쵰?•쵱?Concrete (grades M10–M80)쵲?•쵳?Steel (Fe415/500/550/000)쵴?•쵵?Structural Sections (ISMB/ ISMC/ ISWB/ PEB tapered)쵶?•쵷?Soil (various unit weights/ friction angles)
촊•촚Masonry (brick/ block)촪Section Properties촺•쵊Standard Rolled Sections쵚•쵪Custom PEB Sections (tapered)쵺•춊RC Sections (rectangular/ circular/ T-beam)춚•촐?Plate thicknesses/ shell properties촑?촒촓?촔?0 3 5  Loading Entities촕?Load Type촖?Description촗?Dead Load촘?Self weight/ wall loads/ ?oor loads촙?Live Load촠?Imposed loads (IS 875 Part 2)촡?Wind Load촢?IS 875 Part 3촣?Seismic Load촤?IS 1833촥?Snow Load촦?IS 875 Part 4촧?Temperature Load촨?Thermal e?ects촩?Settlement Load촰?Foundation settlement촱?Construction Load촲?Temporary loads촳?Earth Pressure촴?Retaining wall/ RE wall촵?Water Pressure촶?Tanks/ underground structures촷?Each load has:촸?•촹?Load Case쵀?•쵁?Load Combination쵂?•쵃?Design Scenario쵄?•쵅?Applicable entity IDs쵆?쵇쵈?쵉?0 4  RELATIONSHIP MODEL (GRAPH + HIERARCHICAL)쵐?A modern structural system is neither purely hierarchical nor purely relational  We use a hybrid graph-relational MER 쵑?쵒쵓?쵔?0 4 1  Hierarchical relationships (Tree)쵕?Project  쵖? └┒┒ Sites  쵗?     └┒┒ Buildings  쵘?         └┒┒ Floors  쵙?             └┒┒ Spaces  쵠?                 └┒┒ Architectural walls  쵡?쵢쵣?쵤?0 4 2  Graph relationships (Network)쵥?Node ?--+ Element쵦?Beam ?--+ Column ?--+ Slab ?--+ Wall ?--+ Footing쵧?Frames ?--+ Load Cases ?--+ Materials쵨?Every element is linked by:쵩?•쵰?Spatial link = which nodes it connects to쵱?•쵲?Support link = which support/foundation it rests on쵳?•쵴?Load link = which load/combination is applied

촊PART 7 — LOAD ENGINE ARCHITECTURE촚A Uni?ed, Code-Compliant, Extensible, Multi-Structure Loading System촪?쵊쵚7 1 Purpose of the Load Engine쵪The Load Engine is the system that:쵺1 춊Collects user inputs A derived con?guration(Building type/ location/ geometry/ purpose/ occupancy/ soil data/ roof type/ layout )춚2 촐?Generates all necessary load cases A combinations as per relevant codes:촑?o촒?IS 875 (Parts 1–5) for Indian projects촓?o촔?IS 1833 for seismic촕?o촖?IRC/ AASHTO/ Eurocode/ UBC/ IBC/ ASCE/ etc  for global users촗?o촘?Special modules for:촙?▪촠?Land?lls (unit weight/ surcharge/ leachate/ wind over exposed dump)촡?▪촢?Retaining walls (earth pressure/ hydrodynamic/ live surcharge)촣?▪촤?RE walls (pullout forces/ connection loads)촥?▪촦?PEB (wind loads on frames/ cladding pressures/ suction zones)촧?▪촨?Industrial buildings (crane loads/ hanging loads/ mezzanine)촩?▪촰?Water tanks (hydrostatic + hydrodynamic)촱?▪촲?Solar structures (panel loads + wind + ballast)촳?3 촴?Converts loads into analysis-ready formatsFor whichever solver is selected:촵?o촶?Kratos Multiphysics (preferred per your latest instruction)촷?o촸?FEniCSx (optional future backend)촹?o쵀?OpenSeesPy (legacy fallback)쵁?4 쵂?Stores loads in a uni?ed data structure (UDM-Load) 쵃?쵄쵅?쵆?7 2 Architectural Philosophy쵇?The Load Engine must satisfy three fundamental principles:쵈?(1) Universality쵉?Should support any structure:쵐?•쵑?RCC building (G+2/ multi-storey)쵒?•쵓?PEB / steel warehouses쵔?•쵕?Industrial shed with cranes쵖?•쵗?Land?lls쵘?•쵙?Retaining walls쵠?•쵡?RE walls쵢?•쵣?Tanks쵤?•쵥?Bridges (future module)쵦?•쵧?Compound walls쵨?•쵩?Telecom towers쵰?•쵱?Solar plants쵲?(2) Auto-generation based on location쵳?The User inputs simply:쵴?“G+2 RCC building in Hyderabad”쵵?The system automatically pulls:
촊•촚Wind zone/ basic wind speed촪•촺Seismic zone/ soil type/ importance factor쵊•쵚Snow/ if applicable쵪•쵺Terrain category춊•춚Altitude correction촐?•촑?Cladding pressure zones촒?•촓?Dead load library (SSR-linked densities)촔?(3) Solver-agnostic/ but fully compatible촕?Loads generated are converted into:촖?•촗?Kratos Loads json촘?•촙?UF formulation inputs촠?•촡?Streamlit visualization촢?•촣?Internal UDM촤?촥촦?촧?7 3 Inputs to the Load Engine촨?7 3 1 Mandatory location inputs촩?Parameter촰?Description촱?Country촲?India/ GCC/ Europe/ USA/ etc 촳?State/City촴?To fetch wind/seismic zones촵?Soil Type촶?Rock/ Medium/ Soft촷?Elevation촸?For wind corrections촹?Land use쵀?Terrain category쵁?7 3 2 Structural system inputs쵂?Category쵃?Examples쵄?Building type쵅?RCC/ PEB/ Steel frame쵆?Roof type쵇?Sheeted/ concrete/ curved/ truss쵈?Wall type쵉?Masonry/ sheeting/ RCC쵐?Storeys쵑?G+2/ G+5 etc 쵒?Building usage쵓?Residential/ Industrial/ Warehouse쵔?7 3 3 Geometry inputs쵕?•쵖?Plan dimensions쵗?•쵘?Heights쵙?•쵠?Bay spacings쵡?•쵢?Column layout쵣?•쵤?Staircase position쵥?•쵦?Load-bearing vs RCC framed쵧?7 3 4 Material-based auto-loads쵨?•쵩?RCC density쵰?•쵱?Steel density쵲?•쵳?Brickwork쵴?•쵵?Flooring + ?nishes쵶?•쵷?False ceiling + services쵸?쵹춀?춁?7 4 Load Types Supported
촊7 4 1 Dead Loads (DL)촚DL = Material density × volumeAuto-generation from SSR / CPWD / prede?ned material library 촪Examples:촺•쵊RCC slab: 25 kN/m³쵚•쵪Brick wall: 20 kN/m³쵺•춊Floor ?nishes: 1 5 kN/m²춚•촐?Roo?ng sheet: 0 15–0 20 kN/m²촑?7 4 2 Imposed Loads (LL)촒?Per IS 875 Part 2 or other country standards촓?•촔?Residential ?oors: 2 0–3 0 kN/m²촕?•촖?Corridors: 4 0 kN/m²촗?•촘?Industrial ?oors: 5–20 kN/m²촙?•촠?Mezzanine dynamic factors촡?•촢?Crane surge/ crane vertical/ crane tractive loads촣?7 4 3 Wind Loads (WL)촤?Per IS 875 Part 3 (2015)Wind pressure generation:촥?•촦?Basic wind speed촧?•촨?k1/ k2/ k3/ k4 factors촩?•촰?Terrain category촱?•촲?Height variation촳?•촴?Cladding pressure map촵?•촶?PEB wind suction zones (A/ B/ C/ D/ E/ F)촷?Outputs include:촸?•촹?Surface pressures쵀?•쵁?Frame reactions쵂?•쵃?Equivalent nodal loads쵄?•쵅?Windward/leeward pressure쵆?•쵇?Internal pressure쵈?쵉쵐?쵑?7 4 4 Seismic Loads (EL)쵒?Per IS 1833 (Part 1) 2010쵓?Inputs:쵔?•쵕?Zone factor쵖?•쵗?Soil type쵘?•쵙?Importance factor쵠?•쵡?Response reduction factor쵢?•쵣?Damping쵤?•쵥?Modal combination (SRSS/CQC)쵦?Outputs:쵧?•쵨?Storey shear쵩?•쵰?Storey drift쵱?•쵲?Modal participation쵳?•쵴?Equivalent lateral loads쵵?•쵶?Base shear쵷?•쵸?Load distribution ratio

촊PART 3 — ANALYSIS ENGINE (SOLVER CORE) — FULL PRD촚Uni?ed Multi-Solver Analysis Framework for Buildings, Industrial Structures, Land?lls, and Civil Systems촪?쵊쵚3 1 Objective of the Analysis Engine쵪The Analysis Engine is the numerical heart of the system Its job is to convert:쵺•춊User inputs춚•촐?Drawings촑?•촒?Generated parametric models촓?•촔?Uploaded sketches촕?•촖?Selected templates촗?•촘?Architecture-based auto-models촙?→ into a fully solvable 3D model/ capable of:촠?•촡?Static analysis촢?•촣?Linear A nonlinear analysis촤?•촥?Modal/dynamic analysis촦?•촧?Pushover촨?•촩?Soil–structure interaction촰?•촱?Temperature/creep/shrinkage촲?•촳?Fluid A thermal simulations (where relevant)촴?•촵?Large deformation analysis (retaining walls/ land?lls)촶?The engine must support multiple solvers:촷?Primary Solver (default)촸?✔ Kratos Multiphysics (chosen by you) — ideal for:촹?•쵀?Structural Mechanics쵁?•쵂?Geo-mechanics (retaining walls/ land?lls/ slopes)쵃?•쵄?Concrete A Steel constitutive models쵅?•쵆?Nonlinear FEM쵇?•쵈?Coupled multi-physics (optional future upgrade)쵉?Secondary / Optional Backends쵐?The system will allow plug-in solvers:쵑?•쵒?FEniCSx – academic-grade FEM쵓?•쵔?OpenSees – structural/dynamics쵕?•쵖?Code_Aster – high-?delity EU-grade쵗?•쵘?STAAD import/export – compatibility layer쵙?•쵠?ETABS/SAP model export – optional future upgrade쵡?All solvers are wrapped behind a Uni?ed Analysis API so the UI and work?ows never depend on any single solver 쵢?쵣쵤?쵥?3 2 Uni?ed Analysis API쵦?Every solver follows one common interface:쵧?3 2 1 Core Methods쵨?1 쵩?build_model(structural_model)Converts UDM → element mesh → loads/boundary conditions → solver-ready format 
촊2 촚run_static(gravity + live + wind + seismic)Produce:촪o촺Node displacements쵊o쵚Member forces (axial/ shear/ bending)쵪o쵺Stress ?eld춊o춚Reactions촐?3 촑?run_modal()촒?o촓?Natural periods촔?o촕?Mode shapes촖?o촗?Participation factors촘?4 촙?run_response_spectrum(IS 1833 / ASCE 7 / EC8)촠?5 촡?run_pushover()촢?0 촣?run_thermal() (future update)촤?7 촥?run_geotechnical() (retaining wall/ RE wall/ land?ll)촦?8 촧?export_results()Standard results for design A drawings 촨?3 2 2 Output Format촩?Results shall follow a strict schema:촰?•촱?Displacements (UX/ UY/ UZ)촲?•촳?Rotations (RX/ RY/ RZ)촴?•촵?Member Forces (Fx/ Fy/ Fz/ Mx/ My/ Mz)촶?•촷?Section Stress/Strain촸?•촹?Soil pressures / contact reactions쵀?•쵁?Plastic hinge formation (if nonlinear)쵂?•쵃?Crack width (RCC)쵄?•쵅?Buckling factors (steel frames)쵆?Stored in:쵇?•쵈?SQLite for session쵉?•쵐?JSON for API쵑?•쵒?Parquet for fast large-data storage쵓?쵔쵕?쵖?3 3 Kratos Multiphysics Integration (Primary Engine)쵗?The engine container includes:쵘?Kratos Modules Needed쵙?Module쵠?Purpose쵡?StructuralMechanicsApplication쵢?Steel/RCC frames/ slabs/ beams쵣?GeoMechanicsApplication쵤?Land?lls/ slope stability/ RE walls쵥?FluidDynamicsApplication쵦?(future) wind/?uid simulation쵧?PFEM2Application쵨?Soil–structure interaction쵩?ConstitutiveModelsApplication쵰?Concrete nonlinearity쵱?ContactStructuralMechanics쵲?Retaining walls/ footing-soil contact쵳?Capabilities Enabled쵴?✔ Nonlinear geometry✔ Nonlinear material✔ Reinforced concrete constitutive laws

촊PART 10 — DESIGN ENGINE (MULTI-CODE/ MULTI-MATERIAL) — DETAILED SPECIFICATION촚This section de?nes the core design engine that converts the analyzed structural model into code-compliant member design/ connection design/ foundation design/ and reinforcement detailing 촪The engine must be fully modular/ extendable/ deterministic/ transparent/ and auditable—capable of producing outputs acceptable to Indian Authorities/ including GHMC/ HMDA/ Panchayat Raj/ PWD/ Industrial Local Bodies/ Fire Dept/ PMC/Consultants/ Banks/Financiers/ etc 촺The design engine is the backbone of the system/ responsible for transforming geometry + loads + user intent into actionable engineering designs 쵊?쵪쵺10 1 PURPOSE OF THE DESIGN ENGINE춊The design engine shall:춚1 촐?Interpret the solved FEM model (from Kratos/FEniCSx) 촑?2 촒?Extract forces/ stresses/ reactions/ modal results/ etc 촓?3 촔?Classify members (beams/ columns/ rafters/ joists/ plates/ walls/ footings) 촕?4 촖?Apply design code logic based on:촗?o촘?IS 450/ IS 800/ IS 801촙?o촠?IS 875 (all parts)촡?o촢?IS 1833촣?o촤?IRC/ IS 3370촥?o촦?ACI 318/ AISC 300/ Eurocode 2/3/8 (optional)촧?5 촨?Perform section checks (strength + serviceability) 촩?0 촰?Perform connection design using appropriate code rules 촱?7 촲?Generate reinforcement / steel detailing 촳?8 촴?Generate auto-layout and drawings (Part 12 A 13) 촵?3 촶?Create a structured design report:촷?o촸?Machine readable (JSON)촹?o쵀?Human readable (PDF)쵁?o쵂?“Handwritten Calcs” style formatted for authorities쵃?쵄쵅?쵆?10 2 ARCHITECTURAL PRINCIPLES쵇?10 2 1 Modular쵈?Each design module must be isolated:쵉?design/쵐?  steel/쵑?     is800/쵒?     aisc/쵓?     eurocode3/쵔?  rcc/쵕?     is450/쵖?     is13320/쵗?     is3370/쵘?  foundations/쵙?  connections/쵠?  stairs/
촊  retaining_walls/촚  re_walls/촪  slabs/촺  footings/쵊  raft/쵚10 2 2 Code Polymorphism쵪Same input → Di?erent code rules depending on country/standard:쵺beam design(code="IS800")춊beam design(code="AISC")춚beam design(code="EC3")촐?10 2 3 Deterministic + Auditable촑?•촒?Every calculation must be reversible to step-by-step formula view 촓?•촔?Auto-generated “black box” formulas not allowed 촕?•촖?The user can see:촗?o촘?governing clause촙?o촠?formula촡?o촢?substituted values촣?o촤?result촥?o촦?pass/fail촧?This is mandatory for approving authorities 촨?촩촰?촱?10 3 INPUTS TO DESIGN ENGINE촲?A  From FE Solver촳?•촴?Nx/ Vy/ Vz/ Mx/ My/ Mz for each 1D element촵?•촶?Plate forces: Nx/ Ny/ Nxy/ Mx/ My/ Mxy촷?•촸?Stress tensors촹?•쵀?Reaction forces쵁?•쵂?De?ections쵃?•쵄?Mode shapes (optional)쵅?B  From User쵆?•쵇?Preferred materials A grades쵈?•쵉?Design codes쵐?•쵑?Serviceability limits쵒?•쵓?Fire requirements쵔?•쵕?Crack width/de?ection limits쵖?•쵗?Maximum rebar diameters / steel section libraries쵘?•쵙?Foundation system type preference쵠?C  From Internal Library쵡?•쵢?Steel shapes database (Indian + International)쵣?•쵤?Concrete rebar database쵥?•쵦?Material properties쵧?•쵨?Soil SBC library쵩?•쵰?Bolt/ weld/ anchor bolt databases쵱?쵲쵳?쵴?10 4 DESIGN WORKFLOW쵵?1  Member Recognition쵶?The system must automatically recognize:

촊   !촚 PART 13 — DRAWING A DETAILING ENGINE (DDE)촪(Architectural, Structural, Services, Reinforcement, Steel GA & Fabrication Drawings, and 3D Visual Documentation)촺This section de?nes how your application will automatically generate all drawings required for submission/ construction/ fabrication/ and approvals — based on user inputs/ AI-interpreted layouts/ and engineering design outputs 쵊?쵪쵺13 1 PURPOSE OF THE DRAWING A DETAILING ENGINE춊The DDE is responsible for:춚A  Producing machine-readable/ editable drawings촐?•촑?Architectural plans/ sections/ elevations촒?•촓?Structural framing plans A schedules촔?•촕?RCC reinforcement drawings촖?•촗?Steel GA drawings촘?•촙?Steel fabrication drawings촠?•촡?Staircase/Water tank/Retaining wall/Plinth beam/Compound wall drawings촢?•촣?MEP/Services routing (optional phase)촤?B  Auto-generating drawings from the 3D model촥?Includes:촦?•촧?Automatic views (plan/ section/ elevation/ isometric)촨?•촩?Annotated dimensions촰?•촱?Member IDs/ marks/ bar bending schedules촲?•촳?Optimization-aware member labeling촴?•촵?Clash-free detailing based on BIM/3D geometry촶?C  Multi-format delivery촷?Your app must export in:촸?•촹?DWG쵀?•쵁?DXF쵂?•쵃?PDF쵄?•쵅?SVG쵆?•쵇?3D glTF viewer쵈?•쵉?IFC model export (for interoperability)쵐?D  User-controlled editing쵑?Engineers can:쵒?•쵓?View drawings in browser쵔?•쵕?Select layers (grids/ beams/ columns/ doors)쵖?•쵗?Modify dimensions쵘?•쵙?Move nodes/members쵠?•쵡?Add/delete members쵢?•쵣?Export updated geometry to analysis쵤?Exactly like STAAD + Tekla hybrid functionality 쵥?쵦쵧?쵨?13 2 INPUTS TO DRAWING ENGINE쵩?1 쵰?User Inputs쵱?o쵲?Type of building (G+2/ industrial shed/ RCC framed structure/ warehouse/ etc )쵳?o쵴?User’s chosen layout or uploaded hand sketch/plan

촊   !촚 PART 17 — PLUGIN SYSTEM A EXTENSIBILITY ARCHITECTURE촪A core subsystem enabling modular expansion, custom code modules, third-party engineering engines, AI micro-features, and organization-speci?c work?ows.촺?쵚쵪17 1 Overview A Purpose쵺The Plugin A Extension System (PES) transforms the platform from a ?xed/ monolithic engineering tool into a modular/ extensible/ con?gurable/ and integrable structural engineering ecosystem 춊The purpose of PES is to allow:춚•촐?Structural engineers to add new member types/ materials/ design codes/ and checks 촑?•촒?Software teams to integrate external solvers (Kratos/ FEniCSx/ OpenSeesPy/ Abaqus/ SAP2000/ ETABS/ STAAD) 촓?•촔?AI teams to add AI-powered modular work?ows such as:촕?o촖?Image → Floor plan extraction촗?o촘?Hand sketch → Editable model촙?o촠?Voice → Structural input촡?o촢?Document ingestion → Requirements parser촣?•촤?Companies to implement:촥?o촦?Internal QA rules촧?o촨?SOP-based design work?ows촩?o촰?Custom report formats촱?o촲?Custom bill of quantities templates촳?•촴?Universities / training programs to create:촵?o촶?Educational plug-ins촷?o촸?Validation modules촹?o쵀?Work?ows for learning concepts쵁?This architecture future-proofs the platform by enabling rapid addition of features without changing the core application 쵂?쵃쵄?쵅?17 2 Architectural Principles쵆?1 쵇?IsolationEach plugin runs in a sandboxed environment (VM or isolated container) to ensure security 쵈?2 쵉?Loose CouplingPlugins interact with the core engine via well-de?ned APIs 쵐?3 쵑?Zero-Core Modi?cationNo plugins are allowed to modify core ?les  All extension is via:쵒?o쵓?Events쵔?o쵕?Hooks쵖?o쵗?Plugin API쵘?o쵙?Safe scripting sandbox쵠?4 쵡?Version-SafePlugin compatibility is tracked:쵢?o쵣?App version쵤?o쵥?API version쵦?o쵧?Data schema version

촊It transforms the platform into a structural engineering OS rather than just a tool 촚PART 18 – RESOURCE OPTIMIZATION ENGINE촪A Core Intelligence Layer for Labour, Material, Equipment, Takt Planning & AI-Driven Construction E?iciency촺?쵚쵪18 1 Purpose of the Module쵺The Resource Optimization Engine (ROE) is the system’s intelligence layer responsible for:춊•춚Optimal selection and scheduling of labour/ materials/ equipment/ and construction resources 촐?•촑?Minimizing cost/ duration/ rework/ downtime/ and idle time 촒?•촓?Automatically generating optimized project sequences and takt plans 촔?•촕?Ensuring resource alignment with design outputs/ BoQs/ rates/ and availability 촖?•촗?Providing alternative solutions in case of shortages/ delays/ price changes/ or design modi?cations 촘?This module acts as the “brain” behind overall construction execution/ connecting:촙?•촠?Design → Quantities → Costing → Procurement → Execution Planning → Site Work?ow → Monitoring → Revision Cycle 촡?It must operate across all structure types supported by the platform:PEB/ RCC/ steel structures/ industrial buildings/ retaining walls/ RE walls/ land?lls/ warehouses/ G+2 buildings/ and future expansions 촢?촣촤?촥?18 2 Core Objectives촦?1 촧?Predict Optimal Resource MixUsing engineering quantities + productivity norms + SSR/DSR + market rates 촨?2 촩?Minimize Project DurationThrough dynamic scheduling/ constraint satisfaction/ and AI-driven sequencing 촰?3 촱?Optimize CostAchieve lowest cost without compromising safety/ quality/ or compliance 촲?4 촳?Remove Human Scheduling BiasesAuto-generate realistic and e?icient plans based on target completion timeline 촴?5 촵?Simulation Before ExecutionWhat-if scenarios for:촶?o촷?manpower variation/촸?o촹?equipment availability/쵀?o쵁?cash-?ow constraints/쵂?o쵃?multiple subcontractor performance pro?les 쵄?0 쵅?Auto-Adjust PlansBased on:쵆?o쵇?real-time site progress/쵈?o쵉?supply chain delays/쵐?o쵑?weather events/쵒?o쵓?design revisions 쵔?쵕쵖?쵗?18 3 Inputs to the Module쵘?18 3 촊   !촚 PART 13 — SECURITY/ DATA INTEGRITY A COMPLIANCE FRAMEWORK촪(For the AI-Driven Structural Design, Estimation, and Project Management Platform)촺?쵚쵪13 1 Purpose쵺This section establishes the security/ integrity/ compliance/ governance/ and operational safety rules that must be followed across the entire platform — from architectural planning to design/ estimation/ project execution/ document management/ and closure  The intent is:춊•춚To protect user data/ drawings/ models/ design ?les/ SSR rates/ project estimates/ and proprietary engineering logic 촐?•촑?To ensure compliance with IS codes/ IT standards/ data-privacy protocols/ and audit requirements 촒?•촓?To guarantee that all generated designs/ calculations/ and outputs are tamper-proof/ veri?able/ traceable/ and audit-ready 촔?This applies to all modules — Architecture/ Structural Design/ Kratos/FEniCSx Simulation Layer/ Drawing Engine/ Estimation/ Billing/ QA/QC/ PMC/ Procurement/ and Execution work?ows 촕?촖촗?촘?13 2 Core Security Principles촙?13 2 1 Zero-Trust Architecture촠?•촡?Every user request is authenticated 촢?•촣?Every design operation is veri?ed 촤?•촥?No module trusts another module without explicit token-based permission 촦?13 2 2 Principle of Least Privilege (PoLP)촧?Each engineer or contractor only sees:촨?•촩?Their projects촰?•촱?Their permitted modules촲?•촳?Their allowed design tools촴?•촵?Their billing-activated services촶?13 2 3 Defense-in-Depth촷?Security is layered at:촸?•촹?UI → API → Microservices → Solver Engine → Database → Storage → Deployment → Backup쵀?13 2 4 Tamper-Proof Engineering Output쵁?All engineering outputs must include:쵂?•쵃?Auto-generated calculation IDs쵄?•쵅?SHA-250 hash signatures쵆?•쵇?Version stamps쵈?•쵉?Author + AI model + date + code references쵐?쵑쵒?쵓?13 3 Authentication A Authorization쵔?13 3 1 Multi-Layer Auth쵕?Supported modes:쵖?•쵗?Password + Email OTP쵘?•쵙?OAuth: Google/ Microsoft쵠?•쵡?SSO: Enterprise (SAML2 0)쵢?•쵣?Optional MFA: TOTP / SMS
촊13 3 2 RBAC (Role Based Access Control)촚Roles include:촪•촺Owner / Admin쵊•쵚Structural Engineer쵪•쵺Architect춊•춚Estimator촐?•촑?Site Engineer촒?•촓?Project Manager촔?•촕?Procurement촖?•촗?Client / Viewer촘?•촙?Reviewer / Approver촠?Each role has access rules prede?ned in the ACL dictionary 촡?13 3 3 Project-Level Permissions촢?•촣?View Model촤?•촥?Modify Model촦?•촧?Run Structural Solver (Kratos/FEniCSx)촨?•촩?Generate Drawings촰?•촱?Issue Documents촲?•촳?Download Reports촴?•촵?Approve / Reject촶?•촷?Modify Cost Data촸?•촹?Upload Sketch / Plan쵀?•쵁?Access AI drafting tools쵂?쵃쵄?쵅?13 4 Data Integrity Requirements쵆?13 4 1 Versioning쵇?Every ?le (drawing/ model/ calculation sheet) must maintain:쵈?•쵉?Version number쵐?•쵑?Change description쵒?•쵓?Editor identity쵔?•쵕?Date/time쵖?•쵗?Comparison di? view쵘?13 4 2 Immutable Design Vault쵙?Once a design is "Approved":쵠?•쵡?It becomes read-only쵢?•쵣?Only new revisions can be created쵤?•쵥?All revisions must maintain history lineage tracking쵦?13 4 3 Design Chain of Custody쵧?Each model action is recorded:쵨?•쵩?Node added/removed쵰?•쵱?Member edited쵲?•쵳?Loads updated쵴?•쵵?Meshing updated쵶?•쵷?Solver iterations쵸?•쵹?Code compliance checks춀?•춁?Drawing regenerated춂?All logs stored in a secure audit database

촊   !촚 PART 23 — SYSTEM-WIDE INTELLIGENCE LAYER (SWIL)촪AI-Powered Reasoning/ Learning/ and Cross-Module Orchestration촺This part de?nes the brain of the entire platform — the layer that understands user intent/ orchestrates work?ows/ extracts engineering meaning from sketches and drawings/ recommends optimizations/ validates compliance/ anticipates missing inputs/ learns from previous projects/ and assists engineers throughout design/ estimation/ planning/ execution/ and closure 쵊This is a mandatory component enabling the platform to behave like a virtual structural engineer + architect + estimator + project manager 쵚?쵺춊23 1 Purpose of the System-Wide Intelligence Layer (SWIL)춚SWIL ensures that the platform moves beyond “manual model-building” and becomes a guided/ semi-autonomous engineering system/ capable of:촐?1  Understanding user intent촑?•촒?“I want a G+2 building in Hyderabad”촓?•촔?“I need a 20m clear-span industrial shed”촕?•촖?“I want to check stability of an RE Wall”촗?•촘?“I only want estimation; skip design”촙?2  Asking follow-up questions촠?Automatically generates structured dialogs:촡?•촢?Soil pro?le,촣?•촤?Site location (to get wind/seismic),촥?•촦?Loads (live/ dead/ machinery/ storage),촧?•촨?Usage type (residential/industrial/commercial),촩?3  Mapping user intent → Engineering modules촰?•촱?Architectural → Space planning engine촲?•촳?Structural → Framing system identi?cation촴?•촵?Geotechnical → Soil A foundation module촶?•촷?Estimation → SSR-driven rate analysis촸?•촹?Drawings → 2D + 3D Generator쵀?•쵁?Work?ow → Project lifecycle generator쵂?4  Reducing manual modelling through automation쵃?•쵄?Suggests column grids쵅?•쵆?Suggests best-?t framing layouts쵇?•쵈?Suggests PEB or RCC depending on span/economy쵉?•쵐?Auto-detects missing inputs and requests them쵑?5  Real-time engineering validation쵒?•쵓?Detects under/over-designed members쵔?•쵕?Warns about IS 875/IS 450/IS 1833 non-compliance쵖?•쵗?Validates architectural → structural consistency쵘?•쵙?QA/QC rule engine for every module쵠?0  End-to-end process orchestration쵡?•쵢?From input → layout → model → design → drawings → BOQ → execution plan쵣?•쵤?Allows skipping stages (e g / estimation only)쵥?쵦쵧?쵨?23 2 SWIL Architecture Overview쵩? ┑┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┒┐

촊   !촚 PART 30 — FAILURE MODES/ SAFETY CHECKS A ENGINEERING VALIDATION ENGINE촪This section de?nes the built-in system responsible for identifying/ ?agging/ and quantifying structural failures/ serviceability violations/ constructability risks/ and code non-compliances across all supported structure types (RCC/ Steel/ PEB/ Composite/ Land?lls/ Retaining Walls/ RE Walls/ Bridges/ Industrial Sheds/ Warehouses/ etc ) 촺The Failure Modes A Validation Engine must operate independently of the design engine and must be capable of:쵊1 쵚Stand-alone post-processing (for models imported from STAAD/ Etabs/ SAP2000/ Robot/ Tekla/ or any other tool) 쵪2 쵺Inline real-time checks while the user is modelling in the app#s 2D/3D editor 춊3 춚Batch validation for multiple models in automated work?ows (AI-driven) 촐?촑촒?촓?30 1 Purpose A Objectives촔?The engine must:촕?•촖?Detect unsafe design conditions 촗?•촘?Identify code violations as per IS / IRC / ACI / AISC / Eurocode 촙?•촠?Evaluate serviceability failures (de?ection/ crack width/ drift/ settlement) 촡?•촢?Provide failure-speci?c recommendations 촣?•촤?Give numerical/ graphical/ and AI-explanatory feedback 촥?•촦?Prevent user from proceeding to drawing generation if critical failures exist 촧?•촨?Log failure history for quality audits and certi?cation 촩?촰촱?촲?30 2 Supported Codes촳?Indian Codes (Primary)촴?•촵?IS 450촶?•촷?IS 800촸?•촹?IS 801쵀?•쵁?IS 875 Parts 1–5쵂?•쵃?IS 1833쵄?•쵅?IS 10700쵆?•쵇?IS 2350 (Foundations)쵈?•쵉?IS 3370 (Water tanks)쵐?•쵑?IS 13320 (Ductile detailing)쵒?•쵓?IS 14458 (Retaining/RE walls)쵔?•쵕?IRC 0/ IRC 21 (Bridge components)쵖?•쵗?SWM 2010 (Land?lls)쵘?•쵙?CPHEEO Manual (Land?lls A STP/Water infra)쵠?International Codes (Secondary)쵡?•쵢?AISC LRFD쵣?•쵤?ACI 318쵥?•쵦?EN 1332/ 1333/ 1337/ 1338쵧?•쵨?ASCE 7쵩?•쵰?FHWA (For RE walls)쵱?쵲쵳?쵴?30 3 Failure Mode Categories쵵?The engine must group failures into 7 master categories:
촊?촪촺Category 1: Strength (Ultimate Limit State) Failures쵊Applicable to RCC/ Steel/ Composite A Foundations 쵚Checks include:쵪•쵺Flexure capacity exceeded춊•춚Shear/diagonal tension failure촐?•촑?Bond A anchorage failure촒?•촓?Bearing stress exceedance촔?•촕?Buckling (local A global)촖?•촗?Torsion failure촘?•촙?Combined axial + bending + shear failures촠?•촡?Plastic hinge concentration limits촢?•촣?Punching shear (slabs/ footings)촤?•촥?Plate/shell membrane ruptures촦?•촧?Steel member limit state failures (IS 800 Cl  8 A 3)촨?Outputs:촩?•촰?Failure ratio촱?•촲?Governing load combination촳?•촴?Governing location (element ID/ node ID)촵?•촶?Recommended redesign steps촷?촸촹?쵀?Category 2: Serviceability Failures (SLS)쵁?Includes:쵂?•쵃?Excess vertical de?ection쵄?•쵅?Excess lateral drift쵆?•쵇?Crack width violation쵈?•쵉?Vibration frequencies below acceptable thresholds쵐?•쵑?Di?erential settlement쵒?•쵓?Opening distortion쵔?Outputs:쵕?•쵖?Code-referenced limits쵗?•쵘?Measured values쵙?•쵠?Recommended sizing changes쵡?쵢쵣?쵤?Category 3: Stability Failures쵥?Includes:쵦?•쵧?Global structural instability쵨?•쵩?Local buckling (steel/web/?ange)쵰?•쵱?Lateral-torsional buckling쵲?•쵳?P-Delta e?ects쵴?•쵵?Soil bearing failure쵶?•쵷?Slope instability (Land?ll)쵸?•쵹?RE wall sliding/overturning/pullout/connection failure춀?춁춂?춃?Category 4: Constructability Failures춄?Includes:춅?•춆?Reinforcement congestion

PART 30 — ADVANCED SAFETY ENGINE A CODE COMPLIANCE MODULE쵸?(Next major section of the PRD)쵹?30 1 Overview

촊PART 43 — ADVANCED AI-ASSISTED MODEL VALIDATION A CORRECTION ENGINE촚43 1 Purpose A Scope촪This module ensures that every structural model—whether user-created/ AI-generated/ imported from STAAD/ETABS/Revit/ or sketched—is validated/ corrected/ optimized/ and made design-ready automatically 촺The system becomes the “intelligent checker” that performs:쵊•쵚Automatic model sanity checks쵪•쵺AI-driven correction of geometry/ loads/ supports/ connectivity춊•춚Suggestions for improving design safety/ cost/ constructability촐?•촑?Compliance checks against IS/ACI/AISC/EuroCodes촒?•촓?Generation of layer-by-layer warnings and proposed ?xes촔?•촕?Real-time validation while the Engineer edits the 3D model촖?•촗?A continuous quality assurance AI loop촘?•촙?Prevention of common design failures촠?This eliminates rework/ reduces errors/ and ensures that models coming from any source become clean/ analysable FEA-ready models 촡?촢촣?촤?43 2 Key Responsibilities of This Module촥?1  Geometry Validation촦?•촧?Detect:촨?o촩?Duplicate nodes촰?o촱?Coincident nodes not merged촲?o촳?Members with zero length촴?o촵?Unconnected beams/columns촶?o촷?Orphaned elements촸?o촹?Inconsistent boundary conditions쵀?•쵁?Provide a map of geometric issues:쵂?o쵃?Severity: Critical / Major / Minor쵄?o쵅?Location in 3D model쵆?o쵇?Recommended correction쵈?2  Load Validation쵉?•쵐?Check:쵑?o쵒?Load cases completeness (DL/ LL/ WL/ EQ)쵓?o쵔?Missing tributary areas쵕?o쵖?Wrongly assigned loads쵗?o쵘?Illogical combinations (e g / EQ without mass)쵙?o쵠?Inconsistent wind direction/orientation쵡?•쵢?Suggest improvements:쵣?o쵤?Auto-generate IS 875 loads쵥?o쵦?Auto-generate IS 1833 load patterns쵧?o쵨?Auto-generate snow/ drift/ ponding loads쵩?o쵰?Auto-generate moving loads (if required)쵱?3  Material A Section Checks쵲?•쵳?Detect:쵴?o쵵?Missing material de?nitions쵶?o쵷?Wrong material in elements (e g / RCC slab as steel)쵸?o쵹?Unsupported section naming
